             <h3 id="introduction">Introduction</h3>
-            <p>Android developers, like most developers, are lazy and do not want to write a bunch of code which looks like this:</p>
-            <pre class="prettyprint">class ExampleActivity extends Activity {
-  TextView title;
-  TextView subtitle;
-  TextView footer;
-
-  @Override public void onCreate(Bundle savedInstanceState) {
-    super.onCreate(savedInstanceState);
-    setContentView(R.layout.simple_activity);
-    title = (TextView) findViewById(R.id.title);
-    subtitle = (TextView) findViewById(R.id.subtitle);
-    footer = (TextView) findViewById(R.id.footer);
-
-    // TODO Use views...
-  }
-}</pre>
-            <p>Instead, they turn to helper libraries that they likely do not fully understand. These libraries might use annotations and magic to allow you to condense your code to:</p>
-            <pre class="prettyprint">class ExampleActivity extends Activity {
-  @Magic(R.id.title) TextView title;
-  @Magic(R.id.subtitle) TextView subtitle;
-  @Magic(R.id.footer) TextView footer;
-
-  @Override public void onCreate(Bundle savedInstanceState) {
-    super.onCreate(savedInstanceState);
-    setContentView(R.layout.simple_activity);
-    // TODO Use "injected" views...
-  }
-}</pre>
-            <p>While it looks pretty, magic is for children (and it also comes with a heavy runtime penalty).</p>
-            <p>Instead we can leverage a powerful part of the <code>javac</code> compiler to generate the first example's <code>findViewById</code> boilerplate while still allowing us to keep the terseness of the annotations:</p>
+            <p>Annotate fields with <code>@InjectView</code> and a view ID for Butter Knife to find and automatically cast the corresponding view in your layout.</p>
             <pre class="prettyprint">class ExampleActivity extends Activity {
   @InjectView(R.id.title) TextView title;
   @InjectView(R.id.subtitle) TextView subtitle;
@@ -65,13 +37,13 @@ <h3 id="introduction">Introduction</h3>
     // TODO Use "injected" views...
   }
 }</pre>
-            <p>In place of magic we now call an <code>inject</code> method. This method delegates to generated code that you can see and debug:</p>
+            <p>Instead of slow reflection, code is generated to perform the view look-ups. Calling <code>inject</code> delegates to this generated code that you can see and debug.</p>
+            <p>The generated code for the above example is roughly equivalent to the following:</p>
             <pre class="prettyprint">public void inject(ExampleActivity activity) {
   activity.subtitle = (android.widget.TextView) activity.findViewById(2130968578);
   activity.footer = (android.widget.TextView) activity.findViewById(2130968579);
   activity.title = (android.widget.TextView) activity.findViewById(2130968577);
 }</pre>
-            <p>Some people call this view injection and lump it along with traditional dependency injection frameworks. They may be wrong in nomenclature, but perhaps there exists some use for it.</p>

             <p>You can also perform injection on arbitrary objects by supplying your own view root.</p>

+            <h4 id="view-lists">View Lists</h4>
+            <p>You can group multiple views into a <code>List</code> or array.</p>
+            <pre class="prettyprint">@InjectViews({ R.id.first_name, R.id.middle_name, R.id.last_name })
+List&lt;EditText> nameViews;</pre>
+            <p>The <code>apply</code> method allows you to act on all the views in a list at once.</p>
+            <pre class="prettyprint">ButterKnife.apply(nameViews, DISABLE);
+ButterKnife.apply(nameViews, ENABLED, false);</pre>
+            <p><code>Action</code> and <code>Setter</code> interfaces allow specifying simple behavior.</p>
+            <pre class="prettyprint">static final Action&lt;View> DISABLE = new Action&lt;>() {
+  @Override public void apply(View view, int index) {
+    view.setEnabled(false);
+  }
+}
+static final Setter&lt;View, Boolean> ENABLED = new Setter&lt;>() {
+  @Override public void set(View view, Boolean value, int index) {
+    view.setEnabled(value);
+  }
+}</pre>
+            <p>An Android <a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/util/Property.html"><code>Property</code></a> can also be used with the <code>apply</code> method.</p>
+            <pre class="prettyprint">ButterKnife.apply(nameViews, View.ALPHA, 0);</pre>
+
             <h4 id="click-injection">Click Listener Injection</h4>
             <p>Click listeners can also automatically be configured onto methods.</p>
             <pre class="prettyprint">@OnClick(R.id.submit)
@@ -171,6 +164,18 @@ <h4 id="optional">Optional Injections</h4>
   // TODO ...
 }</pre>
 
+            <h4 id="multi-method-listeners">Multi-Method Listeners</h4>
+            <p>Method annotations whose corresponding listener has multiple callbacks can be used to bind to any one of them. Each annotation has a default callback that it binds to. Specify an alternate using the <code>callback</code> parameter.</p>
+            <pre class="prettyprint">@OnItemSelected(R.id.list_view)
+void onItemSelected(int position) {
+  // TODO ...
+}
+
+@OnItemSelected(value = R.id.maybe_missing, callback = NOTHING_SELECTED)
+void onNothingSelected() {
+  // TODO ...
+}</pre>
+
             <h4 id="bonus">Bonus</h4>
             <p>Also included are two <code>findById</code> methods which simplify code that still has to find views on a <code>View</code> or <code>Activity</code>. It uses generics to infer the return type and automatically performs the cast.</p>
             <pre class="prettyprint">View view = LayoutInflater.from(context).inflate(R.layout.thing, null);
@@ -193,6 +198,17 @@ <h4>Maven</h4>
   &lt;version><span class="version"><em>(insert latest version)</em></span>&lt;/version>
 &lt;/dependency></pre>
 
+            <h4>Gradle</h4>
+            <pre class="prettyprint">compile 'com.jakewharton:butterknife:<span class="version"><em>(insert latest version)</em></span>'</pre>
+            <p>Be sure to supress this lint warning in your <code>build.gradle</code>.</p>
+            <pre class="prettyprint">lintOptions {
+  disable 'InvalidPackage'
+}</pre>
+            <p>Some configurations may also require additional exclusions.</p>
+            <pre class="prettyprint">packagingOptions {
+  exclude 'META-INF/services/javax.annotation.processing.Processor'
+}</pre>
+

+<h2 title="Interface ButterKnife.Action" class="title">Interface ButterKnife.Action&lt;T extends android.view.View&gt;</h2>
+</div>

-Class ButterKnife</H2>
-<PRE>
-<A HREF="http://java.sun.com/javase/6/docs/api/java/lang/Object.html?is-external=true" title="class or interface in java.lang">java.lang.Object</A>

-</PRE>
-<HR>
-<DL>
-<DT><PRE>public class <B>ButterKnife</B><DT>extends <A HREF="http://java.sun.com/javase/6/docs/api/java/lang/Object.html?is-external=true" title="class or interface in java.lang">Object</A></DL>
-</PRE>
-
-<P>
-View injection utilities. Use this class to simplify finding views and attaching listeners by
+<div class="header">
+<div class="subTitle">butterknife</div>
+<h2 title="Class ButterKnife" class="title">Class ButterKnife</h2>
+</div>
+<div class="contentContainer">
+<ul class="inheritance">
+<li>java.lang.Object</li>
+<li>
+<ul class="inheritance">
+<li>butterknife.ButterKnife</li>
+</ul>
+</li>
+</ul>
+<div class="description">
+<ul class="blockList">
+<li class="blockList">
+<hr>
+<br>
+<pre>public final class <span class="typeNameLabel">ButterKnife</span>
+extends java.lang.Object</pre>
+<div class="block">View "injection" utilities. Use this class to simplify finding views and attaching listeners by
  injecting them.
  <p>
  Injecting views from your activity is as easy as:
  <pre><code>
  public class ExampleActivity extends Activity {
-   @InjectView(R.id.title) EditText titleView;
-   @InjectView(R.id.subtitle) EditText subtitleView;
+    @InjectView(R.id.title) EditText titleView;
+    @InjectView(R.id.subtitle) EditText subtitleView;
 
-   @Override protected void onCreate(Bundle savedInstanceState) {
+    @Override protected void onCreate(Bundle savedInstanceState) {
      super.onCreate(savedInstanceState);
      setContentView(R.layout.example_activity);
      ButterKnife.inject(this);
    }
  }
  </code></pre>
- You can inject an <A HREF="../butterknife/ButterKnife.html#inject(android.app.Activity)"><CODE>activity directly</CODE></A> or a <A HREF="../butterknife/ButterKnife.html#inject(android.view.View)"><CODE>view
- directly</CODE></A>, or inject an <A HREF="../butterknife/ButterKnife.html#inject(java.lang.Object, android.app.Activity)"><CODE>activity into another object</CODE></A> or a
- <A HREF="../butterknife/ButterKnife.html#inject(java.lang.Object, android.view.View)"><CODE>view into another object</CODE></A>.
+ You can inject an <a href="../butterknife/ButterKnife.html#inject-android.app.Activity-">activity directly</a> or a<a href="../butterknife/ButterKnife.html#inject-android.view.View-">view directly</a>, or inject an <a href="../butterknife/ButterKnife.html#inject-java.lang.Object-android.app.Activity-">activity into another object</a>
+ or a <a href="../butterknife/ButterKnife.html#inject-java.lang.Object-android.view.View-">view into another object</a>.
+ <p>
+ Group multiple views together into a <code>List</code> or array.
+ <pre><code>
+  @InjectViews({R.id.first_name, R.id.middle_name, R.id.last_name})
+ List<EditText> nameViews;
+ </code></pre>
+ There are three convenience methods for working with view collections:
+ <ul>
+ <li><a href="../butterknife/ButterKnife.html#apply-java.util.List-butterknife.ButterKnife.Action-"><code>apply(List, Action)</code></a> &ndash; Applies an action to each view.</li>
+ <li><a href="../butterknife/ButterKnife.html#apply-java.util.List-butterknife.ButterKnife.Setter-V-"><code>apply(List, Setter, Object)</code></a> &ndash; Applies a setter value to each view.</li>
+ <li><a href="../butterknife/ButterKnife.html#apply-java.util.List-android.util.Property-V-"><code>apply(List, Property, Object)</code></a> &ndash; Applies a property value to each view.</li>
+ </ul>
  <p>
  To inject listeners to your views you can annotate your methods:
  <pre><code>
- @OnClick(R.id.submit) void onSubmit() {
+  @OnClick(R.id.submit) void onSubmit() {
    // React to button click.
  }
  </code></pre>
  Any number of parameters from the listener may be used on the method.
  <pre><code>
- @OnItemClick(R.id.tweet_list) void onTweetClicked(int position) {
+  @OnItemClick(R.id.tweet_list) void onTweetClicked(int position) {
    // React to tweet click.
  }
  </code></pre>
  <p>
  Be default, views are required to be present in the layout for both field and method injections.
- If a view is optional add the <A HREF="../butterknife/Optional.html" title="annotation in butterknife"><CODE>@Optional</CODE></A> annotation.
+ If a view is optional add the <a href="../butterknife/Optional.html" title="annotation in butterknife"><code>@Optional</code></a> annotation.
  <pre><code>
- @Optional @InjectView(R.id.title) TextView subtitleView;
- </code></pre>
-<P>
-
-<P>
-<DL>
-<DT><B>See Also:</B><DD><A HREF="../butterknife/InjectView.html" title="annotation in butterknife"><CODE>InjectView</CODE></A>,

-<A HREF="../butterknife/OnLongClick.html" title="annotation in butterknife"><CODE>OnLongClick</CODE></A></DL>

+  @Optional @InjectView(R.id.title) TextView subtitleView;
+ </code></pre></div>

-<H2>
-<FONT SIZE="-1">
-butterknife</FONT>
-<BR>
-Annotation Type InjectView</H2>
-<HR>
-<DL>
-<DT><PRE><FONT SIZE="-1"><A HREF="http://java.sun.com/javase/6/docs/api/java/lang/annotation/Retention.html?is-external=true" title="class or interface in java.lang.annotation">@Retention</A>(<A HREF="http://java.sun.com/javase/6/docs/api/java/lang/annotation/Retention.html?is-external=true#value()" title="class or interface in java.lang.annotation">value</A>=<A HREF="http://java.sun.com/javase/6/docs/api/java/lang/annotation/RetentionPolicy.html?is-external=true#CLASS" title="class or interface in java.lang.annotation">CLASS</A>)
-<A HREF="http://java.sun.com/javase/6/docs/api/java/lang/annotation/Target.html?is-external=true" title="class or interface in java.lang.annotation">@Target</A>(<A HREF="http://java.sun.com/javase/6/docs/api/java/lang/annotation/Target.html?is-external=true#value()" title="class or interface in java.lang.annotation">value</A>=<A HREF="http://java.sun.com/javase/6/docs/api/java/lang/annotation/ElementType.html?is-external=true#FIELD" title="class or interface in java.lang.annotation">FIELD</A>)
-</FONT>public @interface <B>InjectView</B></DL>
-</PRE>
-
-<P>
-Annotation for fields which indicate that it should be looked up in the view or activity layout.
- The view will automatically be cast to the field type.
+<div class="header">
+<div class="subTitle">butterknife</div>
+<h2 title="Annotation Type InjectView" class="title">Annotation Type InjectView</h2>
+</div>
+<div class="contentContainer">
+<div class="description">
+<ul class="blockList">
+<li class="blockList">
+<hr>
+<br>
+<pre>@Retention(value=CLASS)
+ @Target(value=FIELD)
+public @interface <span class="memberNameLabel">InjectView</span></pre>
+<div class="block">Bind a field to the view for the specified ID. The view will automatically be cast to the field
+ type.
  <pre><code>
- @InjectView(R.id.title) TextView title;
- </code></pre>
-<P>
-
-<P>
-<DL>
-<DT><B>See Also:</B><DD><A HREF="../butterknife/Optional.html" title="annotation in butterknife"><CODE>Optional</CODE></A></DL>
-<HR>
-
-<P>
+  @InjectView(R.id.title) TextView title;
+ </code></pre></div>
+<dl>
+<dt><span class="seeLabel">See Also:</span></dt>
+<dd><a href="../butterknife/Optional.html" title="annotation in butterknife"><code>Optional</code></a></dd>
+</dl>
+</li>
+</ul>
+</div>
+<div class="summary">
+<ul class="blockList">
+<li class="blockList">

+<!-- ======== START OF CLASS DATA ======== -->
+<div class="header">
+<div class="subTitle">butterknife</div>
+<h2 title="Annotation Type InjectViews" class="title">Annotation Type InjectViews</h2>
+</div>
+<div class="contentContainer">
+<div class="description">
+<ul class="blockList">
+<li class="blockList">
+<hr>
+<br>
+<pre>@Retention(value=CLASS)
+ @Target(value=FIELD)
+public @interface <span class="memberNameLabel">InjectViews</span></pre>
+<div class="block">Bind a field to the view for each ID specified in a <code>List</code> or array. Each view will
+ automatically be cast to the list or array type.
+ <pre><code>
+  @InjectViews({R.id.first_name, R.id.middle_name, R.id.last_name})
+ List&lt;TextView&gt; nameViews;
+
+  @InjectViews({R.id.address_line_1, R.id.address_line_2})
+ EditText[] addressViews;
+ </code></pre></div>
+</li>
+</ul>
+</div>
+<div class="summary">
+<ul class="blockList">
+<li class="blockList">
+<!-- =========== ANNOTATION TYPE REQUIRED MEMBER SUMMARY =========== -->
+<ul class="blockList">
+<li class="blockList"><a name="annotation.type.required.element.summary">
+<!--   -->
+</a>
+<h3>Required Element Summary</h3>
+<table class="memberSummary" border="0" cellpadding="3" cellspacing="0" summary="Required Element Summary table, listing required elements, and an explanation">
+<caption><span>Required Elements</span><span class="tabEnd">&nbsp;</span></caption>
+<tr>
+<th class="colFirst" scope="col">Modifier and Type</th>
+<th class="colLast" scope="col">Required Element and Description</th>
+</tr>
+<tr class="altColor">
+<td class="colFirst"><code>int[]</code></td>

-<H2>
-<FONT SIZE="-1">
-butterknife</FONT>
-<BR>
-Annotation Type OnCheckedChanged</H2>
-<HR>
-<DL>
-<DT><PRE><FONT SIZE="-1"><A HREF="http://java.sun.com/javase/6/docs/api/java/lang/annotation/Retention.html?is-external=true" title="class or interface in java.lang.annotation">@Retention</A>(<A HREF="http://java.sun.com/javase/6/docs/api/java/lang/annotation/Retention.html?is-external=true#value()" title="class or interface in java.lang.annotation">value</A>=<A HREF="http://java.sun.com/javase/6/docs/api/java/lang/annotation/RetentionPolicy.html?is-external=true#CLASS" title="class or interface in java.lang.annotation">CLASS</A>)
-<A HREF="http://java.sun.com/javase/6/docs/api/java/lang/annotation/Target.html?is-external=true" title="class or interface in java.lang.annotation">@Target</A>(<A HREF="http://java.sun.com/javase/6/docs/api/java/lang/annotation/Target.html?is-external=true#value()" title="class or interface in java.lang.annotation">value</A>=<A HREF="http://java.sun.com/javase/6/docs/api/java/lang/annotation/ElementType.html?is-external=true#METHOD" title="class or interface in java.lang.annotation">METHOD</A>)
-<A HREF="../butterknife/internal/ListenerClass.html" title="annotation in butterknife.internal">@ListenerClass</A>(<A HREF="../butterknife/internal/ListenerClass.html#value()">value</A>="android.widget.CompoundButton.OnCheckedChangeListener")
-</FONT>public @interface <B>OnCheckedChanged</B></DL>
-</PRE>
-
-<P>
-Annotation for methods which indicate that they should be called when a view is checked or
- unchecked. Corresponds to adding a <CODE>CompoundButton.OnCheckedChangeListener</CODE> to the views specified by
- <A HREF="../butterknife/OnCheckedChanged.html#value()"><CODE>value()</CODE></A>.
+<div class="header">
+<div class="subTitle">butterknife</div>
+<h2 title="Annotation Type OnCheckedChanged" class="title">Annotation Type OnCheckedChanged</h2>
+</div>
+<div class="contentContainer">
+<div class="description">
+<ul class="blockList">
+<li class="blockList">
+<hr>
+<br>
+<pre>@Target(value=METHOD)
+ @Retention(value=CLASS)
+public @interface <span class="memberNameLabel">OnCheckedChanged</span></pre>
+<div class="block">Bind a method to an <code>OnCheckedChangeListener</code> on the view for
+ each ID specified.
  <pre><code>
- @OnCheckedChanged(R.id.example) void onChecked(boolean checked) {
+  @OnCheckedChanged(R.id.example) void onChecked(boolean checked) {
    Toast.makeText(this, checked ? "Checked!" : "Unchecked!", LENGTH_SHORT).show();
  }
  </code></pre>
- Any number of parameters from <CODE>CompoundButton.OnCheckedChangeListener</CODE> may be used on the method.
-<P>
-
-<P>
-<DL>
-<DT><B>See Also:</B><DD><CODE>CompoundButton.OnCheckedChangeListener</CODE>, 
-<A HREF="../butterknife/Optional.html" title="annotation in butterknife"><CODE>Optional</CODE></A></DL>
-<HR>
-
-<P>
+ Any number of parameters from
+ <code>onCheckedChanged</code> may be used on the method.</div>
+<dl>
+<dt><span class="seeLabel">See Also:</span></dt>
+<dd><code>CompoundButton.OnCheckedChangeListener</code>, 
+<a href="../butterknife/Optional.html" title="annotation in butterknife"><code>Optional</code></a></dd>
+</dl>
+</li>
+</ul>
+</div>
+<div class="summary">
+<ul class="blockList">
+<li class="blockList">

-<H2>
-<FONT SIZE="-1">
-butterknife</FONT>
-<BR>
-Annotation Type OnClick</H2>
-<HR>
-<DL>
-<DT><PRE><FONT SIZE="-1"><A HREF="http://java.sun.com/javase/6/docs/api/java/lang/annotation/Retention.html?is-external=true" title="class or interface in java.lang.annotation">@Retention</A>(<A HREF="http://java.sun.com/javase/6/docs/api/java/lang/annotation/Retention.html?is-external=true#value()" title="class or interface in java.lang.annotation">value</A>=<A HREF="http://java.sun.com/javase/6/docs/api/java/lang/annotation/RetentionPolicy.html?is-external=true#CLASS" title="class or interface in java.lang.annotation">CLASS</A>)
-<A HREF="http://java.sun.com/javase/6/docs/api/java/lang/annotation/Target.html?is-external=true" title="class or interface in java.lang.annotation">@Target</A>(<A HREF="http://java.sun.com/javase/6/docs/api/java/lang/annotation/Target.html?is-external=true#value()" title="class or interface in java.lang.annotation">value</A>=<A HREF="http://java.sun.com/javase/6/docs/api/java/lang/annotation/ElementType.html?is-external=true#METHOD" title="class or interface in java.lang.annotation">METHOD</A>)
-<A HREF="../butterknife/internal/ListenerClass.html" title="annotation in butterknife.internal">@ListenerClass</A>(<A HREF="../butterknife/internal/ListenerClass.html#value()">value</A>="android.view.View.OnClickListener")
-</FONT>public @interface <B>OnClick</B></DL>
-</PRE>
-
-<P>
-Annotation for methods which indicate that they should be called when a view is clicked.
- Corresponds to adding a <CODE>View.OnClickListener</CODE> to the views specified by <A HREF="../butterknife/OnClick.html#value()"><CODE>value()</CODE></A>.
+<div class="header">
+<div class="subTitle">butterknife</div>
+<h2 title="Annotation Type OnClick" class="title">Annotation Type OnClick</h2>
+</div>
+<div class="contentContainer">
+<div class="description">
+<ul class="blockList">
+<li class="blockList">
+<hr>
+<br>
+<pre>@Target(value=METHOD)
+ @Retention(value=CLASS)
+public @interface <span class="memberNameLabel">OnClick</span></pre>
+<div class="block">Bind a method to an <code>OnClickListener</code> on the view for each ID specified.
  <pre><code>
- @OnClick(R.id.example) void onClick() {
+  @OnClick(R.id.example) void onClick() {
    Toast.makeText(this, "Clicked!", LENGTH_SHORT).show();
  }
  </code></pre>
- Any number of parameters from <CODE>View.OnClickListener</CODE> may be used on the method.
-<P>
-
-<P>
-<DL>
-<DT><B>See Also:</B><DD><CODE>View.OnClickListener</CODE>, 
-<A HREF="../butterknife/Optional.html" title="annotation in butterknife"><CODE>Optional</CODE></A></DL>
-<HR>
-
-<P>
+ Any number of parameters from
+ <code>onClick</code> may be used on the
+ method.</div>
+<dl>
+<dt><span class="seeLabel">See Also:</span></dt>
+<dd><code>View.OnClickListener</code>, 
+<a href="../butterknife/Optional.html" title="annotation in butterknife"><code>Optional</code></a></dd>
+</dl>
+</li>
+</ul>
+</div>
+<div class="summary">
+<ul class="blockList">
+<li class="blockList">

-<H2>
-<FONT SIZE="-1">
-butterknife</FONT>
-<BR>
-Annotation Type OnEditorAction</H2>
-<HR>
-<DL>
-<DT><PRE><FONT SIZE="-1"><A HREF="http://java.sun.com/javase/6/docs/api/java/lang/annotation/Retention.html?is-external=true" title="class or interface in java.lang.annotation">@Retention</A>(<A HREF="http://java.sun.com/javase/6/docs/api/java/lang/annotation/Retention.html?is-external=true#value()" title="class or interface in java.lang.annotation">value</A>=<A HREF="http://java.sun.com/javase/6/docs/api/java/lang/annotation/RetentionPolicy.html?is-external=true#CLASS" title="class or interface in java.lang.annotation">CLASS</A>)
-<A HREF="http://java.sun.com/javase/6/docs/api/java/lang/annotation/Target.html?is-external=true" title="class or interface in java.lang.annotation">@Target</A>(<A HREF="http://java.sun.com/javase/6/docs/api/java/lang/annotation/Target.html?is-external=true#value()" title="class or interface in java.lang.annotation">value</A>=<A HREF="http://java.sun.com/javase/6/docs/api/java/lang/annotation/ElementType.html?is-external=true#METHOD" title="class or interface in java.lang.annotation">METHOD</A>)
-<A HREF="../butterknife/internal/ListenerClass.html" title="annotation in butterknife.internal">@ListenerClass</A>(<A HREF="../butterknife/internal/ListenerClass.html#value()">value</A>="android.widget.TextView.OnEditorActionListener")
-</FONT>public @interface <B>OnEditorAction</B></DL>
-</PRE>
-
-<P>
-Annotation for methods which indicate that they should be called when an edit action occurs.
- Corresponds to adding a <CODE>TextView.OnEditorActionListener</CODE> to the views specified by
- <A HREF="../butterknife/OnEditorAction.html#value()"><CODE>value()</CODE></A>.
+<div class="header">
+<div class="subTitle">butterknife</div>
+<h2 title="Annotation Type OnEditorAction" class="title">Annotation Type OnEditorAction</h2>
+</div>
+<div class="contentContainer">
+<div class="description">
+<ul class="blockList">
+<li class="blockList">
+<hr>
+<br>
+<pre>@Target(value=METHOD)
+ @Retention(value=CLASS)
+public @interface <span class="memberNameLabel">OnEditorAction</span></pre>
+<div class="block">Bind a method to an <code>OnEditorActionListener</code> on the view for each
+ ID specified.
  <pre><code>
- @OnEditorAction(R.id.example) boolean onEditorAction(KeyEvent key) {
+  @OnEditorAction(R.id.example) boolean onEditorAction(KeyEvent key) {
    Toast.makeText(this, "Pressed: " + key, LENGTH_SHORT).show();
    return true;
  }
  </code></pre>
- Any number of parameters from <CODE>TextView.OnEditorActionListener</CODE> may be used on the method.
-<P>
-
-<P>
-<DL>
-<DT><B>See Also:</B><DD><CODE>TextView.OnEditorActionListener</CODE>, 
-<A HREF="../butterknife/Optional.html" title="annotation in butterknife"><CODE>Optional</CODE></A></DL>
-<HR>
-
-<P>
+ Any number of parameters from
+ <code>onEditorAction</code> may be used on the method.</div>
+<dl>
+<dt><span class="seeLabel">See Also:</span></dt>
+<dd><code>TextView.OnEditorActionListener</code>, 
+<a href="../butterknife/Optional.html" title="annotation in butterknife"><code>Optional</code></a></dd>
+</dl>
+</li>
+</ul>
+</div>
+<div class="summary">
+<ul class="blockList">
+<li class="blockList">

+<div class="header">
+<div class="subTitle">butterknife</div>
+<h2 title="Annotation Type OnFocusChange" class="title">Annotation Type OnFocusChange</h2>
+</div>
+<div class="contentContainer">
+<div class="description">
+<ul class="blockList">
+<li class="blockList">
+<hr>
+<br>
+<pre>@Target(value=METHOD)
+ @Retention(value=CLASS)
+public @interface <span class="memberNameLabel">OnFocusChange</span></pre>
+<div class="block">Bind a method to an <code>OnFocusChangeListener</code> on the view for each ID
+ specified.
+ <pre><code>
+  @OnFocusChanged(R.id.example) void onFocusChanged(boolean focused) {
+   Toast.makeText(this, focused ? "Gained focus" : "Lost focus", LENGTH_SHORT).show();
+ }
+ </code></pre>
+ Any number of parameters from <code>onFocusChange</code> may be used on the method.</div>
+<dl>
+<dt><span class="seeLabel">See Also:</span></dt>
+<dd><code>View.OnFocusChangeListener</code>, 
+<a href="../butterknife/Optional.html" title="annotation in butterknife"><code>Optional</code></a></dd>
+</dl>
+</li>
+</ul>
+</div>
+<div class="summary">
+<ul class="blockList">
+<li class="blockList">
+<!-- =========== ANNOTATION TYPE REQUIRED MEMBER SUMMARY =========== -->
+<ul class="blockList">
+<li class="blockList"><a name="annotation.type.required.element.summary">
+<!--   -->
+</a>

+<table class="memberSummary" border="0" cellpadding="3" cellspacing="0" summary="Required Element Summary table, listing required elements, and an explanation">

+<tr>
+<th class="colFirst" scope="col">Modifier and Type</th>
+<th class="colLast" scope="col">Required Element and Description</th>
+</tr>
+<tr class="altColor">
+<td class="colFirst"><code>int[]</code></td>
+<td class="colLast"><code><span class="memberNameLink"><a href="../butterknife/OnFocusChange.html#value--">value</a></span></code>
+<div class="block">View IDs to which the method will be bound.</div>
+</td>
+</tr>
+</table>
+</li>
+</ul>
+</li>
+</ul>
+</div>

-<FONT SIZE="-1">
-butterknife</FONT>
-<BR>
-Annotation Type OnFocusChanged</H2>
-<HR>
-<DL>
-<DT><PRE><FONT SIZE="-1"><A HREF="http://java.sun.com/javase/6/docs/api/java/lang/annotation/Retention.html?is-external=true" title="class or interface in java.lang.annotation">@Retention</A>(<A HREF="http://java.sun.com/javase/6/docs/api/java/lang/annotation/Retention.html?is-external=true#value()" title="class or interface in java.lang.annotation">value</A>=<A HREF="http://java.sun.com/javase/6/docs/api/java/lang/annotation/RetentionPolicy.html?is-external=true#CLASS" title="class or interface in java.lang.annotation">CLASS</A>)
-<A HREF="http://java.sun.com/javase/6/docs/api/java/lang/annotation/Target.html?is-external=true" title="class or interface in java.lang.annotation">@Target</A>(<A HREF="http://java.sun.com/javase/6/docs/api/java/lang/annotation/Target.html?is-external=true#value()" title="class or interface in java.lang.annotation">value</A>=<A HREF="http://java.sun.com/javase/6/docs/api/java/lang/annotation/ElementType.html?is-external=true#METHOD" title="class or interface in java.lang.annotation">METHOD</A>)
-<A HREF="../butterknife/internal/ListenerClass.html" title="annotation in butterknife.internal">@ListenerClass</A>(<A HREF="../butterknife/internal/ListenerClass.html#value()">value</A>="android.view.View.OnFocusChangeListener")
-</FONT>public @interface <B>OnFocusChanged</B></DL>
-</PRE>
-
-<P>
-Annotation for methods which indicate that they should be called when a view's focus changed.
- Corresponds to adding a <CODE>View.OnFocusChangeListener</CODE> to the views specified by <A HREF="../butterknife/OnFocusChanged.html#value()"><CODE>value()</CODE></A>.
- <pre><code>
- @OnFocusChanged(R.id.example) void onFocusChanged(boolean focused) {
-   Toast.makeText(this, focused ? "Gained focus" : "Lost focus", LENGTH_SHORT).show();
- }
- </code></pre>
- Any number of parameters from <CODE>View.OnFocusChangeListener</CODE> may be used on the method.
-<P>
-
-<P>
-<DL>
-<DT><B>See Also:</B><DD><CODE>View.OnFocusChangeListener</CODE>, 
-<A HREF="../butterknife/Optional.html" title="annotation in butterknife"><CODE>Optional</CODE></A></DL>
-<HR>
-

-<H2>
-<FONT SIZE="-1">
-butterknife</FONT>
-<BR>
-Annotation Type OnItemClick</H2>
-<HR>
-<DL>
-<DT><PRE><FONT SIZE="-1"><A HREF="http://java.sun.com/javase/6/docs/api/java/lang/annotation/Retention.html?is-external=true" title="class or interface in java.lang.annotation">@Retention</A>(<A HREF="http://java.sun.com/javase/6/docs/api/java/lang/annotation/Retention.html?is-external=true#value()" title="class or interface in java.lang.annotation">value</A>=<A HREF="http://java.sun.com/javase/6/docs/api/java/lang/annotation/RetentionPolicy.html?is-external=true#CLASS" title="class or interface in java.lang.annotation">CLASS</A>)
-<A HREF="http://java.sun.com/javase/6/docs/api/java/lang/annotation/Target.html?is-external=true" title="class or interface in java.lang.annotation">@Target</A>(<A HREF="http://java.sun.com/javase/6/docs/api/java/lang/annotation/Target.html?is-external=true#value()" title="class or interface in java.lang.annotation">value</A>=<A HREF="http://java.sun.com/javase/6/docs/api/java/lang/annotation/ElementType.html?is-external=true#METHOD" title="class or interface in java.lang.annotation">METHOD</A>)
-<A HREF="../butterknife/internal/ListenerClass.html" title="annotation in butterknife.internal">@ListenerClass</A>(<A HREF="../butterknife/internal/ListenerClass.html#value()">value</A>="android.widget.AdapterView.OnItemClickListener")
-</FONT>public @interface <B>OnItemClick</B></DL>
-</PRE>
-
-<P>
-Annotation for methods which indicate that they should be called when an item is clicked.
- Corresponds to adding a <CODE>AdapterView.OnItemClickListener</CODE> to the views specified by <A HREF="../butterknife/OnItemClick.html#value()"><CODE>value()</CODE></A>.
+<div class="header">
+<div class="subTitle">butterknife</div>
+<h2 title="Annotation Type OnItemClick" class="title">Annotation Type OnItemClick</h2>
+</div>
+<div class="contentContainer">
+<div class="description">
+<ul class="blockList">
+<li class="blockList">
+<hr>
+<br>
+<pre>@Target(value=METHOD)
+ @Retention(value=CLASS)
+public @interface <span class="memberNameLabel">OnItemClick</span></pre>
+<div class="block">Bind a method to an <code>OnItemClickListener</code> on the view for each ID
+ specified.
  <pre><code>
- @OnItemClick(R.id.example_list) void onItemClick(int position) {
+  @OnItemClick(R.id.example_list) void onItemClick(int position) {
    Toast.makeText(this, "Clicked position " + position + "!", LENGTH_SHORT).show();
  }
  </code></pre>
- Any number of parameters from <CODE>AdapterView.OnItemClickListener</CODE> may be used on the method.
-<P>
-
-<P>
-<DL>
-<DT><B>See Also:</B><DD><CODE>AdapterView.OnItemClickListener</CODE>, 
-<A HREF="../butterknife/Optional.html" title="annotation in butterknife"><CODE>Optional</CODE></A></DL>
-<HR>
-
-<P>
+ Any number of parameters from <code>onItemClick</code> may be used on the method.</div>
+<dl>
+<dt><span class="seeLabel">See Also:</span></dt>
+<dd><code>AdapterView.OnItemClickListener</code>, 
+<a href="../butterknife/Optional.html" title="annotation in butterknife"><code>Optional</code></a></dd>
+</dl>
+</li>
+</ul>

-Annotation Type OnItemLongClick</H2>
-<HR>
-<DL>
-<DT><PRE><FONT SIZE="-1"><A HREF="http://java.sun.com/javase/6/docs/api/java/lang/annotation/Retention.html?is-external=true" title="class or interface in java.lang.annotation">@Retention</A>(<A HREF="http://java.sun.com/javase/6/docs/api/java/lang/annotation/Retention.html?is-external=true#value()" title="class or interface in java.lang.annotation">value</A>=<A HREF="http://java.sun.com/javase/6/docs/api/java/lang/annotation/RetentionPolicy.html?is-external=true#CLASS" title="class or interface in java.lang.annotation">CLASS</A>)
-<A HREF="http://java.sun.com/javase/6/docs/api/java/lang/annotation/Target.html?is-external=true" title="class or interface in java.lang.annotation">@Target</A>(<A HREF="http://java.sun.com/javase/6/docs/api/java/lang/annotation/Target.html?is-external=true#value()" title="class or interface in java.lang.annotation">value</A>=<A HREF="http://java.sun.com/javase/6/docs/api/java/lang/annotation/ElementType.html?is-external=true#METHOD" title="class or interface in java.lang.annotation">METHOD</A>)
-<A HREF="../butterknife/internal/ListenerClass.html" title="annotation in butterknife.internal">@ListenerClass</A>(<A HREF="../butterknife/internal/ListenerClass.html#value()">value</A>="android.widget.AdapterView.OnItemLongClickListener")
-</FONT>public @interface <B>OnItemLongClick</B></DL>
-</PRE>
-
-<P>
-Annotation for methods which indicate that they should be called when an item is long pressed.
- Corresponds to adding a <CODE>AdapterView.OnItemLongClickListener</CODE> to the views specified by
- <A HREF="../butterknife/OnItemLongClick.html#value()"><CODE>value()</CODE></A>.
+<div class="header">
+<div class="subTitle">butterknife</div>
+<h2 title="Annotation Type OnItemLongClick" class="title">Annotation Type OnItemLongClick</h2>
+</div>
+<div class="contentContainer">
+<div class="description">
+<ul class="blockList">
+<li class="blockList">
+<hr>
+<br>
+<pre>@Target(value=METHOD)
+ @Retention(value=CLASS)
+public @interface <span class="memberNameLabel">OnItemLongClick</span></pre>
+<div class="block">Bind a method to an <code>OnItemLongClickListener</code> on the view for each
+ ID specified.
  <pre><code>
- @OnItemLongClick(R.id.example_list) boolean onItemLongClick(int position) {
+  @OnItemLongClick(R.id.example_list) boolean onItemLongClick(int position) {
    Toast.makeText(this, "Long clicked position " + position + "!", LENGTH_SHORT).show();
    return true;
  }
  </code></pre>
- Any number of parameters from <CODE>AdapterView.OnItemLongClickListener</CODE> may be used on the method.
-<P>
-
-<P>
-<DL>
-<DT><B>See Also:</B><DD><CODE>AdapterView.OnItemLongClickListener</CODE>, 
-<A HREF="../butterknife/Optional.html" title="annotation in butterknife"><CODE>Optional</CODE></A></DL>
-<HR>
-
-<P>
+ Any number of parameters from
+ <code>onItemLongClick</code> may be used on the method.</div>
+<dl>
+<dt><span class="seeLabel">See Also:</span></dt>
+<dd><code>AdapterView.OnItemLongClickListener</code>, 
+<a href="../butterknife/Optional.html" title="annotation in butterknife"><code>Optional</code></a></dd>
+</dl>
+</li>
+</ul>
+</div>
+<div class="summary">
+<ul class="blockList">
+<li class="blockList">

+<div class="header">
+<div class="subTitle">butterknife</div>
+<h2 title="Annotation Type OnItemSelected" class="title">Annotation Type OnItemSelected</h2>
+</div>
+<div class="contentContainer">
+<div class="description">
+<ul class="blockList">
+<li class="blockList">
+<hr>
+<br>
+<pre>@Target(value=METHOD)
+ @Retention(value=CLASS)
+public @interface <span class="memberNameLabel">OnItemSelected</span></pre>
+<div class="block">Bind a method to an <code>OnItemSelectedListener</code> on the view for each
+ ID specified.
+ <pre><code>
+  @OnItemSelected(R.id.example_list) void onItemSelected(int position) {
+   Toast.makeText(this, "Selected position " + position + "!", LENGTH_SHORT).show();
+ }
+ </code></pre>
+ Any number of parameters from
+ <code>onItemSelected</code> may be used on the method.
+ <p>
+ To bind to methods other than <code>onItemSelected</code>, specify a different <code>callback</code>.
+ <pre><code>
+  @OnItemSelected(value = R.id.example_list, callback = NOTHING_SELECTED)
+ void onNothingSelected() {
+   Toast.makeText(this, "Nothing selected!", LENGTH_SHORT).show();
+ }
+ </code></pre></div>
+<dl>
+<dt><span class="seeLabel">See Also:</span></dt>
+<dd><code>AdapterView.OnItemSelectedListener</code>, 
+<a href="../butterknife/Optional.html" title="annotation in butterknife"><code>Optional</code></a></dd>
+</dl>
+</li>
+</ul>
+</div>
+<div class="summary">
+<ul class="blockList">
+<li class="blockList">
+<!-- =========== ANNOTATION TYPE REQUIRED MEMBER SUMMARY =========== -->

-Annotation Type OnLongClick</H2>

-<DL>
-<DT><PRE><FONT SIZE="-1"><A HREF="http://java.sun.com/javase/6/docs/api/java/lang/annotation/Retention.html?is-external=true" title="class or interface in java.lang.annotation">@Retention</A>(<A HREF="http://java.sun.com/javase/6/docs/api/java/lang/annotation/Retention.html?is-external=true#value()" title="class or interface in java.lang.annotation">value</A>=<A HREF="http://java.sun.com/javase/6/docs/api/java/lang/annotation/RetentionPolicy.html?is-external=true#CLASS" title="class or interface in java.lang.annotation">CLASS</A>)
-<A HREF="http://java.sun.com/javase/6/docs/api/java/lang/annotation/Target.html?is-external=true" title="class or interface in java.lang.annotation">@Target</A>(<A HREF="http://java.sun.com/javase/6/docs/api/java/lang/annotation/Target.html?is-external=true#value()" title="class or interface in java.lang.annotation">value</A>=<A HREF="http://java.sun.com/javase/6/docs/api/java/lang/annotation/ElementType.html?is-external=true#METHOD" title="class or interface in java.lang.annotation">METHOD</A>)
-<A HREF="../butterknife/internal/ListenerClass.html" title="annotation in butterknife.internal">@ListenerClass</A>(<A HREF="../butterknife/internal/ListenerClass.html#value()">value</A>="android.view.View.OnLongClickListener")
-</FONT>public @interface <B>OnLongClick</B></DL>
-</PRE>
-
-<P>
-Annotation for methods which indicate that they should be called when a view is long pressed.
- Corresponds to adding a <CODE>View.OnLongClickListener</CODE> to the views specified by <A HREF="../butterknife/OnLongClick.html#value()"><CODE>value()</CODE></A>.
+<div class="header">
+<div class="subTitle">butterknife</div>
+<h2 title="Annotation Type OnLongClick" class="title">Annotation Type OnLongClick</h2>
+</div>
+<div class="contentContainer">
+<div class="description">
+<ul class="blockList">
+<li class="blockList">
+<hr>
+<br>
+<pre>@Retention(value=CLASS)
+ @Target(value=METHOD)
+public @interface <span class="memberNameLabel">OnLongClick</span></pre>
+<div class="block">Bind a method to an <code>OnLongClickListener</code> on the view for each ID
+ specified.
  <pre><code>
- @OnLongClick(R.id.example) boolean onLongClick() {
+  @OnLongClick(R.id.example) boolean onLongClick() {
    Toast.makeText(this, "Long clicked!", LENGTH_SHORT).show();
    return true;
  }
  </code></pre>
- Any number of parameters from <CODE>View.OnLongClickListener</CODE> may be used on the method.
-<P>
-
-<P>
-<DL>
-<DT><B>See Also:</B><DD><CODE>View.OnLongClickListener</CODE>, 
-<A HREF="../butterknife/Optional.html" title="annotation in butterknife"><CODE>Optional</CODE></A></DL>
-<HR>
-
-<P>
+ Any number of parameters from <code>View.OnLongClickListener.onLongClick(android.view.View)</code> may be
+ used on the method.</div>
+<dl>
+<dt><span class="seeLabel">See Also:</span></dt>
+<dd><code>View.OnLongClickListener</code>, 
+<a href="../butterknife/Optional.html" title="annotation in butterknife"><code>Optional</code></a></dd>
+</dl>
+</li>
+</ul>
+</div>
+<div class="summary">
+<ul class="blockList">
+<li class="blockList">

+<div class="header">
+<div class="subTitle">butterknife</div>
+<h2 title="Annotation Type OnPageChange" class="title">Annotation Type OnPageChange</h2>
+</div>
+<div class="contentContainer">
+<div class="description">
+<ul class="blockList">
+<li class="blockList">
+<hr>
+<br>
+<pre>@Target(value=METHOD)
+ @Retention(value=CLASS)
+public @interface <span class="memberNameLabel">OnPageChange</span></pre>
+<div class="block">Bind a method to an <code>OnPageChangeListener</code> on the view for each ID specified.
+ <pre><code>
+  @OnPageChange(R.id.example_pager) void onPageSelected(int position) {
+   Toast.makeText(this, "Selected " + position + "!", LENGTH_SHORT).show();
+ }
+ </code></pre>
+ Any number of parameters from <code>onPageSelected</code> may be used on the method.
+ <p>
+ To bind to methods other than <code>onPageSelected</code>, specify a different <code>callback</code>.
+ <pre><code>
+  @OnPageChange(value = R.id.example_pager, callback = PAGE_SCROLL_STATE_CHANGED)
+ void onPageStateChanged(int state) {
+   Toast.makeText(this, "State changed: " + state + "!", LENGTH_SHORT).show();
+ }
+ </code></pre></div>
+<dl>
+<dt><span class="seeLabel">See Also:</span></dt>
+<dd><a href="../butterknife/Optional.html" title="annotation in butterknife"><code>Optional</code></a></dd>
+</dl>
+</li>
+</ul>
+</div>
+<div class="summary">
+<ul class="blockList">
+<li class="blockList">
+<!-- =========== ANNOTATION TYPE REQUIRED MEMBER SUMMARY =========== -->

+enum constant in this type.  (Extraneous whitespace characters are 
+not permitted.)</div>
+<dl>
+<dt><span class="paramLabel">Parameters:</span></dt>
+<dd><code>name</code> - the name of the enum constant to be returned.</dd>
+<dt><span class="returnLabel">Returns:</span></dt>
+<dd>the enum constant with the specified name</dd>
+<dt><span class="throwsLabel">Throws:</span></dt>
+<dd><code>java.lang.IllegalArgumentException</code> - if this enum type has no constant with the specified name</dd>
+<dd><code>java.lang.NullPointerException</code> - if the argument is null</dd>
+</dl>
+</li>
+</ul>
+</li>
+</ul>
+</li>
+</ul>
+</div>

+<!-- ======== START OF CLASS DATA ======== -->
+<div class="header">
+<div class="subTitle">butterknife</div>
+<h2 title="Annotation Type OnTextChanged" class="title">Annotation Type OnTextChanged</h2>
+</div>
+<div class="contentContainer">
+<div class="description">
+<ul class="blockList">
+<li class="blockList">
+<hr>
+<br>
+<pre>@Target(value=METHOD)
+ @Retention(value=CLASS)
+public @interface <span class="memberNameLabel">OnTextChanged</span></pre>
+<div class="block">Bind a method to an <code>TextWatcher</code> on the view for each ID specified.
+ <pre><code>
+  @OnTextChanged(R.id.example) void onTextChanged(CharSequence text) {
+   Toast.makeText(this, "Text changed: " + text, LENGTH_SHORT).show();
+ }
+ </code></pre>
+ Any number of parameters from <code>onTextChanged</code> may be used on the method.
+ <p>
+ To bind to methods other than <code>onTextChanged</code>, specify a different <code>callback</code>.
+ <pre><code>
+  @OnTextChanged(value = R.id.example, callback = BEFORE_TEXT_CHANGED)
+ void onBeforeTextChanged(CharSequence text {
+   Toast.makeText(this, "Before text changed: " + text, LENGTH_SHORT).show();
+ }
+ </code></pre></div>
+<dl>
+<dt><span class="seeLabel">See Also:</span></dt>
+<dd><code>TextWatcher</code>, 
+<a href="../butterknife/Optional.html" title="annotation in butterknife"><code>Optional</code></a></dd>
+</dl>
+</li>
+</ul>
+</div>
+<div class="summary">
+<ul class="blockList">
+<li class="blockList">
+<!-- =========== ANNOTATION TYPE REQUIRED MEMBER SUMMARY =========== -->
+<ul class="blockList">
+<li class="blockList"><a name="annotation.type.required.element.summary">

+</tr>

+<td class="colLast"><code><span class="memberNameLink"><a href="../butterknife/OnTextChanged.html#value--">value</a></span></code>

+</td>
+</tr>
+</table>

+<a name="package.description">
+<!--   -->
+</a>
+<h2 title="Package butterknife Description">Package butterknife Description</h2>
+<div class="block">View "injection" library for Android which uses annotation processing to generate boilerplate
+ code for you.
+ <p>
+ <ul>
+ <li>Eliminate <code>findViewById</code> calls by using
+ <a href="../butterknife/InjectView.html" title="annotation in butterknife"><code>@InjectView</code></a> on fields.</li>
+ <li>Group multiple views in a list using
+ <a href="../butterknife/InjectViews.html" title="annotation in butterknife"><code>@InjectViews</code></a>. Operate on all of them at once with
+ <a href="../butterknife/ButterKnife.html#apply-java.util.List-butterknife.ButterKnife.Action-">actions</a>, <a href="../butterknife/ButterKnife.html#apply-java.util.List-butterknife.ButterKnife.Setter-V-">setters</a>, or
+ <a href="../butterknife/ButterKnife.html#apply-java.util.List-android.util.Property-V-">properties</a>.</li>
+ <li>Eliminate anonymous inner-classes for listeners by annotating methods with
+ <a href="../butterknife/OnClick.html" title="annotation in butterknife"><code>@OnClick</code></a> and others.</li>
+ </ul></div>
+</div>

-<HR>
-<CENTER>
-<H1>
-How This API Document Is Organized</H1>
-</CENTER>
-This API (Application Programming Interface) document has pages corresponding to the items in the navigation bar, described as follows.<H3>
-Overview</H3>
-<BLOCKQUOTE>
-
-<P>
-The <A HREF="overview-summary.html">Overview</A> page is the front page of this API document and provides a list of all packages with a summary for each.  This page can also contain an overall description of the set of packages.</BLOCKQUOTE>
-<H3>
-Package</H3>
-<BLOCKQUOTE>
-
-<P>
-Each package has a page that contains a list of its classes and interfaces, with a summary for each. This page can contain four categories:<UL>
-<LI>Interfaces (italic)<LI>Classes<LI>Enums<LI>Exceptions<LI>Errors<LI>Annotation Types</UL>
-</BLOCKQUOTE>
-<H3>
-Class/Interface</H3>
-<BLOCKQUOTE>
-
-<P>
-Each class, interface, nested class and nested interface has its own separate page. Each of these pages has three sections consisting of a class/interface description, summary tables, and detailed member descriptions:<UL>
-<LI>Class inheritance diagram<LI>Direct Subclasses<LI>All Known Subinterfaces<LI>All Known Implementing Classes<LI>Class/interface declaration<LI>Class/interface description
-<P>
-<LI>Nested Class Summary<LI>Field Summary<LI>Constructor Summary<LI>Method Summary
-<P>
-<LI>Field Detail<LI>Constructor Detail<LI>Method Detail</UL>
-Each summary entry contains the first sentence from the detailed description for that item. The summary entries are alphabetical, while the detailed descriptions are in the order they appear in the source code. This preserves the logical groupings established by the programmer.</BLOCKQUOTE>
-</BLOCKQUOTE>
-<H3>
-Annotation Type</H3>
-<BLOCKQUOTE>
-
-<P>
-Each annotation type has its own separate page with the following sections:<UL>
-<LI>Annotation Type declaration<LI>Annotation Type description<LI>Required Element Summary<LI>Optional Element Summary<LI>Element Detail</UL>
-</BLOCKQUOTE>
-</BLOCKQUOTE>
-<H3>
-Enum</H3>
-<BLOCKQUOTE>
-
-<P>
-Each enum has its own separate page with the following sections:<UL>
-<LI>Enum declaration<LI>Enum description<LI>Enum Constant Summary<LI>Enum Constant Detail</UL>
-</BLOCKQUOTE>
-<H3>
-Use</H3>
-<BLOCKQUOTE>
-Each documented package, class and interface has its own Use page.  This page describes what packages, classes, methods, constructors and fields use any part of the given class or package. Given a class or interface A, its Use page includes subclasses of A, fields declared as A, methods that return A, and methods and constructors with parameters of type A.  You can access this page by first going to the package, class or interface, then clicking on the "Use" link in the navigation bar.</BLOCKQUOTE>
-<H3>
-Tree (Class Hierarchy)</H3>
-<BLOCKQUOTE>
-There is a <A HREF="overview-tree.html">Class Hierarchy</A> page for all packages, plus a hierarchy for each package. Each hierarchy page contains a list of classes and a list of interfaces. The classes are organized by inheritance structure starting with <code>java.lang.Object</code>. The interfaces do not inherit from <code>java.lang.Object</code>.<UL>
-<LI>When viewing the Overview page, clicking on "Tree" displays the hierarchy for all packages.<LI>When viewing a particular package, class or interface page, clicking "Tree" displays the hierarchy for only that package.</UL>
-</BLOCKQUOTE>
-<H3>
-Deprecated API</H3>
-<BLOCKQUOTE>
-The <A HREF="deprecated-list.html">Deprecated API</A> page lists all of the API that have been deprecated. A deprecated API is not recommended for use, generally due to improvements, and a replacement API is usually given. Deprecated APIs may be removed in future implementations.</BLOCKQUOTE>
-<H3>
-Index</H3>
-<BLOCKQUOTE>
-The <A HREF="index-all.html">Index</A> contains an alphabetic list of all classes, interfaces, constructors, methods, and fields.</BLOCKQUOTE>
-<H3>
-Prev/Next</H3>
-These links take you to the next or previous class, interface, package, or related page.<H3>
-Frames/No Frames</H3>
-These links show and hide the HTML frames.  All pages are available with or without frames.
-<P>
-<H3>
-Serialized Form</H3>
-Each serializable or externalizable class has a description of its serialization fields and methods. This information is of interest to re-implementors, not to developers using the API. While there is no link in the navigation bar, you can get to this information by going to any serialized class and clicking "Serialized Form" in the "See also" section of the class description.
-<P>
-<H3>
-Constant Field Values</H3>
-The <a href="constant-values.html">Constant Field Values</a> page lists the static final fields and their values.
-<P>
-<FONT SIZE="-1">
-<EM>
-This help file applies to API documentation generated using the standard doclet.</EM>
-</FONT>
-<BR>
-<HR>
-
-
+<div class="header">
+<h1 class="title">How This API Document Is Organized</h1>
+<div class="subTitle">This API (Application Programming Interface) document has pages corresponding to the items in the navigation bar, described as follows.</div>
+</div>
+<div class="contentContainer">
+<ul class="blockList">
+<li class="blockList">
+<h2>Package</h2>
+<p>Each package has a page that contains a list of its classes and interfaces, with a summary for each. This page can contain six categories:</p>
+<ul>
+<li>Interfaces (italic)</li>
+<li>Classes</li>
+<li>Enums</li>
+<li>Exceptions</li>
+<li>Errors</li>
+<li>Annotation Types</li>
+</ul>
+</li>
+<li class="blockList">
+<h2>Class/Interface</h2>
+<p>Each class, interface, nested class and nested interface has its own separate page. Each of these pages has three sections consisting of a class/interface description, summary tables, and detailed member descriptions:</p>
+<ul>
+<li>Class inheritance diagram</li>
+<li>Direct Subclasses</li>
+<li>All Known Subinterfaces</li>
+<li>All Known Implementing Classes</li>
+<li>Class/interface declaration</li>
+<li>Class/interface description</li>
+</ul>
+<ul>
+<li>Nested Class Summary</li>
+<li>Field Summary</li>
+<li>Constructor Summary</li>
+<li>Method Summary</li>
+</ul>
+<ul>
+<li>Field Detail</li>
+<li>Constructor Detail</li>
+<li>Method Detail</li>
+</ul>
+<p>Each summary entry contains the first sentence from the detailed description for that item. The summary entries are alphabetical, while the detailed descriptions are in the order they appear in the source code. This preserves the logical groupings established by the programmer.</p>
+</li>
+<li class="blockList">
+<h2>Annotation Type</h2>
+<p>Each annotation type has its own separate page with the following sections:</p>
+<ul>
+<li>Annotation Type declaration</li>
+<li>Annotation Type description</li>
+<li>Required Element Summary</li>
+<li>Optional Element Summary</li>
+<li>Element Detail</li>
+</ul>
+</li>
+<li class="blockList">
+<h2>Enum</h2>
+<p>Each enum has its own separate page with the following sections:</p>
+<ul>
+<li>Enum declaration</li>
+<li>Enum description</li>
+<li>Enum Constant Summary</li>
+<li>Enum Constant Detail</li>
+</ul>
+</li>
+<li class="blockList">
+<h2>Use</h2>
+<p>Each documented package, class and interface has its own Use page.  This page describes what packages, classes, methods, constructors and fields use any part of the given class or package. Given a class or interface A, its Use page includes subclasses of A, fields declared as A, methods that return A, and methods and constructors with parameters of type A.  You can access this page by first going to the package, class or interface, then clicking on the "Use" link in the navigation bar.</p>
+</li>
+<li class="blockList">
+<h2>Tree (Class Hierarchy)</h2>
+<p>There is a <a href="overview-tree.html">Class Hierarchy</a> page for all packages, plus a hierarchy for each package. Each hierarchy page contains a list of classes and a list of interfaces. The classes are organized by inheritance structure starting with <code>java.lang.Object</code>. The interfaces do not inherit from <code>java.lang.Object</code>.</p>
+<ul>
+<li>When viewing the Overview page, clicking on "Tree" displays the hierarchy for all packages.</li>
+<li>When viewing a particular package, class or interface page, clicking "Tree" displays the hierarchy for only that package.</li>
+</ul>
+</li>
+<li class="blockList">
+<h2>Deprecated API</h2>
+<p>The <a href="deprecated-list.html">Deprecated API</a> page lists all of the API that have been deprecated. A deprecated API is not recommended for use, generally due to improvements, and a replacement API is usually given. Deprecated APIs may be removed in future implementations.</p>
+</li>
+<li class="blockList">
+<h2>Index</h2>
+<p>The <a href="index-all.html">Index</a> contains an alphabetic list of all classes, interfaces, constructors, methods, and fields.</p>
+</li>
+<li class="blockList">
+<h2>Prev/Next</h2>
+<p>These links take you to the next or previous class, interface, package, or related page.</p>
+</li>
+<li class="blockList">
+<h2>Frames/No Frames</h2>
+<p>These links show and hide the HTML frames.  All pages are available with or without frames.</p>
+</li>
+<li class="blockList">
+<h2>All Classes</h2>
+<p>The <a href="allclasses-noframe.html">All Classes</a> link shows all classes and interfaces except non-static nested types.</p>
+</li>
+<li class="blockList">
+<h2>Serialized Form</h2>
+<p>Each serializable or externalizable class has a description of its serialization fields and methods. This information is of interest to re-implementors, not to developers using the API. While there is no link in the navigation bar, you can get to this information by going to any serialized class and clicking "Serialized Form" in the "See also" section of the class description.</p>
+</li>
+<li class="blockList">
+<h2>Constant Field Values</h2>
+<p>The <a href="constant-values.html">Constant Field Values</a> page lists the static final fields and their values.</p>
+</li>
+</ul>
+<span class="emphasizedPhrase">This help file applies to API documentation generated using the standard doclet.</span></div>

diff --git a/javadoc/script.js b/javadoc/script.js
new file mode 100644
index 00000000..b3463569
--- /dev/null
+++ b/javadoc/script.js
@@ -0,0 +1,30 @@
+function show(type)
+{
+    count = 0;
+    for (var key in methods) {
+        var row = document.getElementById(key);
+        if ((methods[key] &  type) != 0) {
+            row.style.display = '';
+            row.className = (count++ % 2) ? rowColor : altColor;
+        }
+        else
+            row.style.display = 'none';
+    }
+    updateTabs(type);
+}
+
+function updateTabs(type)
+{
+    for (var value in tabs) {
+        var sNode = document.getElementById(tabs[value][0]);
+        var spanNode = sNode.firstChild;
+        if (value == type) {
+            sNode.className = activeTableTab;
+            spanNode.innerHTML = tabs[value][1];
+        }
+        else {
+            sNode.className = tableTab;
+            spanNode.innerHTML = "<a href=\"javascript:show("+ value + ");\">" + tabs[value][1] + "</a>";
+        }
+    }
+}
